jdillon 2006-10-31 23:04 #421 Rev.: 469760

Rewrote the module/dependency installation bits, split up into install(), installModule(), installModuleDependencies() and installDependency()
Artifacts are now tracked as they are installed so we can skip them if already processed
When re-installing dependency artifacts we now check the file size and last modified time of the source to determine if it has changed, skipping if it was not
When re-installing modules, we now check all of the module's deps to see if they changed
Default info logging is a bit more verbose now, as it includes the dependency artifacts installed... so you can easily see what was really installed
